                                                            <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                                                <p style="text-align:center">Dr Joy Dental Clinics is an award winning dental clinic group in Dubai which is the largest in the United Arab Emirates. It was established in 2004 and is recognized with the Superbrand award. We have currently Thirteen Dental clinics with more than Hundred highly qualified dentists of different nationalities all committed to delivering excellence in dental care to all our patients for the past 21 years. We provide all the dental services from preventive dentistry to complex full mouth rehabilitation and smile makeover using state of the art technology in a calm and relaxing atmosphere. We also have our own in house dental lab for delivering top notch quality prosthesis. We are looking forward to welcoming you to experience the finest dental care with us.</p>
